# Review Home Base тАФ First Principles Engine

> **What this is:** the single anchor for the Barnes homeschool app's architecture & functional review.
> **Where reviewing happens:** a dedicated Claude.ai chat (the "home base"). It owns the recurring
> audit, holds the live issue ledger, and spins out fix runs.
> **Where fixing happens:** Claude Code web, driven by the prompts in `prompts/`, reviewed before merge.
> **Repo:** github.com/barnes-ngb/first-principles-engine ┬╖ **Live:** first-principles-engine.web.app
> **Created:** 2026-05-29 ┬╖ **Last audit:** 2026-07-12 (`ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-07-12.md`; prior: July 5 run `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-07.md`, June 28 run `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-06-28.md`, June 21 mid-cycle supplement, primary June run: `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-06.md`)

---

## 1. Why this exists

The project already has a working maintenance system (Tiers 1тАУ3 below) that keeps stats and docs
honest every few days. What it lacked was **teeth on architecture** and a path from *finding* to *fix*.
This home base adds that: one recurring deep audit focused on structure and the end-to-end loop, plus
a repeatable fix runner so issues don't just get logged тАФ they get closed.

## 2. Review priority order

Set by Nathan, 2026-05-29. The audit and ledger weight findings in this order:

1. **Architecture & tech debt** тАФ structure, decomposition, bundle, test coverage. *(primary)*
2. **Functional / UX completeness** тАФ does the evaluate тЖТ plan тЖТ execute тЖТ review loop actually work for Shelly and the boys.
3. **Pedagogy & ethos alignment** тАФ charter fidelity, disposition-over-mastery, no-shame, coverage-not-pace.
4. **Data integrity & compliance** тАФ hours aggregation, MO 600-core line, source-of-truth conflicts.

> Note: an item in a lower band still jumps the queue if it is **time-sensitive or compliance-critical**
> (e.g. DATA-01 below, which affects the June 30 MO core-hours line).

## 3. How to run the home base

| Action | Where | How |
|---|---|---|
| **Monthly deep audit** | Claude Code web (scheduled) | Run `prompts/PROMPT_ARCH_AUDIT.md`. Same scheduling mechanism as your /3-day health audit. Suggested: 1st of month, after the health audit. |
| **Fix an issue** | Claude Code web (manual) | Run `prompts/PROMPT_FIX.md` with one issue ID from the ledger (┬з6). |
| **Strategy / triage / "should we even do this"** | Claude.ai home-base chat | Paste this file + the latest dated audit report. Talk it through. Decisions land back in the ledger. |
| **Refresh project context** | Claude.ai project settings | Point the project at `docs/PROJECT_CONTEXT.md` (regenerated weekly by Tier 3), not the stale v14 outline. See DOC-01. |

## 4. The existing maintenance system (unchanged тАФ for reference)

| Tier | Cadence | Output | Owner |
|---|---|---|---|
| **1 тАФ Health Audit** | every 3 days | `docs/HEALTH_REPORT.md` (stats, build/lint/test, doc drift, auto-fixes numbers) | Claude Code scheduled |
| **2 тАФ Fix Companion** | after Tier 1 | auto-fixes mechanical doc gaps (undocumented tasks, missing collections, nav, index) | Claude Code scheduled |
| **3 тАФ Context Gather** | weekly | `docs/PROJECT_CONTEXT.md` (AI-optimized context for design chats) | Claude Code scheduled |
| **4 тАФ Deep Audit** | **monthly (this system)** | dated `docs/review/ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_<YYYY-MM>.md` + ledger update | Home base тЖТ Claude Code |

Tiers 1тАУ3 stay as they are. This home base **is** Tier 4, made concrete.

## 5. Architecture map (as of 2026-05-29)

**Stack:** React + TypeScript + Vite ┬╖ Firebase (Auth/Firestore/Storage/Functions/Hosting) ┬╖ MUI ┬╖
Three.js r128 (3D avatar) ┬╖ Anthropic Claude (Sonnet 4.6 primary, Haiku 4.5 for routine chat) ┬╖
OpenAI gpt-image-1.5 (image generation тАФ migrated from DALL-E 3 + gpt-image-1 per PR #1217).

**Scale (verified against code 2026-06-20):** ~180,429 TS lines ┬╖ 117 commits on main ┬╖
37 Firestore collections ┬╖ 25 Cloud Functions ┬╖ 19 chat task types ┬╖ 34 routes ┬╖ 181 test files ┬╖
2,746 tests passing ┬╖ build/lint/tsc all green.

**The core loop (this is what "functional review" traces):**

```
Evaluate тФАтФАтЦ║ Skill Snapshot тФАтФАтЦ║ Plan My Week тФАтФАтЦ║ Daily checklist (Today) тФАтФАтЦ║ Weekly Review
   тЦ▓              (priority skills,                  (evidence: completion,        тФВ
   тФВ               supports, stop rules,             engagement, mastery,         тФВ
   тФФтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАconceptual blocks)                minutes, artifacts) тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФШ
```

**AI pipeline:** 17 task types dispatched via `functions/src/ai/tasks/` registry; per-task context
slices in `functions/src/ai/contextSlices.ts`; charter preamble injected into all calls.

**Feature homes:** `today/` ┬╖ `planner-chat/` ┬╖ `quest/` (Knowledge Mine) ┬╖ `avatar/` (Hero Hub) ┬╖
`books/` ┬╖ `workshop/` ┬╖ `shelly-chat/` (Ask AI) ┬╖ `evaluate/` ┬╖ `records/` ┬╖ `dad-lab/` ┬╖ `progress/`.

**The central architecture tension (already named in `first-principles-system-review.md`):**
the system can answer *"where is Lincoln right now?"* from **six** places тАФ Skill Snapshot, Ladders,
Milestones, Learning Map, Curriculum position, Disposition profile тАФ and **none is authoritative**.
The loop isn't missing; it has too many overlapping truths. Sharpening that authority is the single
highest-leverage architecture move. Tracked as **FUNC-01**.

## 6. Live issue ledger

Status: `OPEN` ┬╖ `IN PROGRESS` ┬╖ `FIXED` ┬╖ `WONTFIX` ┬╖ `NEEDS-DATA` (requires live Firestore export).
Band = priority band from ┬з2. The audit prompt updates this table; the fix prompt flips status.

**Lanes (ID-prefix legend):** **Structure** тАФ `ARCH` / `TEST` / `LINT` ┬╖ **Functionality** тАФ `FEAT` / `FUNC` ┬╖ **Docs** тАФ `DOC` / `ETHOS` ┬╖ **Data/compliance** тАФ `DATA`.

> **Before appending a row, re-fetch the ledger from `origin/main` and use `max(id)+1` per lane** тАФ concurrent chats can't see each other's pending rows (see the ARCH-18 dup reconciled 2026-06-07, and the bulk dedup of 2026-06-08).

> **Only one ledger-touching run should be in flight at a time across all chats.** Merge it before dispatching the next тАФ `max(id)+1` only protects *sequential* writes; parallel cross-chat appends still collide on the shared counter (the root cause of every duplicate ID swept so far).

> **The avatar / Hero Hub lane uses a distinct `AV-` ID prefix** (`AV-NN`) for its rows going forward, so its appends can't collide with home-base `ARCH-NN`. (Convention for future rows only тАФ existing avatar rows keep their `ARCH-` IDs.)

> **London-specific work lives in `docs/LONDON_BACKLOG.md`, not as `FEAT-` rows.** Per the Lincoln-first /
> London-minimal policy (`CLAUDE.md` тА║ AI Development Operating Model), London touchpoints are tracked
> surface-by-surface in that register to keep this active ledger Lincoln-focused.

| **FUNC-07** | 2 | **FIXED** | **Chapter read section un-break: parent-only chapter skip; skipтЙаanswered; finish = answered-or-skipped; pool visibility; one-time legacy repair.** The kid read-aloud section vanished from both kids' Today after chapters were skipped. Root cause: skipping a chapter wrote `answered:true` (the `answered` flag double-dutied as "answered *or* skipped"), so `useBookProgress` finished the book (`every(answered)`) and `KidTodayView`'s `some(!answered)` gate unmounted the whole section тАФ kids couldn't return to skipped chapters. A flag-guarded one-time migration (`migratedSkipModel`) resets legacy skip-stamped chapters back to answerable (clearing stale `answeredDate`/`responseNote`, dropping `completedAt` when no longer finished) so previously-skipped chapters return; idempotent, scoped to the loaded book, never touches a genuine answer. ## 7. Triggers (phone-first cheat-sheet)

Everything below is either fully automatic or a single short message pasted into Claude Code web.
No local commands, ever.

### Fully automatic (set once)
- **Monthly audit** тАФ scheduled Claude Code task, same as the /3-day health audit. Task prompt:
  > Read `docs/review/prompts/PROMPT_ARCH_AUDIT.md` and execute it fully.

  Suggested schedule: 1st of the month, after the health audit. It auto-applies safe doc fixes and
  opens a PR for everything else. You just review + merge from the phone.

### One-line triggers (paste into Claude Code web on the repo)
- **Run a fix** (you pick the issue ID from ┬з6):
  > Read `docs/review/prompts/PROMPT_FIX.md` and run it for ISSUE_ID: DATA-01

- **Run the audit now** (off-schedule, e.g. before a design session):
  > Read `docs/review/prompts/PROMPT_ARCH_AUDIT.md` and execute it fully.

- **Just triage / ask** (in the Claude.ai home-base chat, not Claude Code):
  > Read REVIEW_HOME_BASE.md and the latest audit report. What should I fix next and why?

### What is and isn't automated (by design)
- **Auto, no touch:** the audit, stat/doc corrections, PR creation.
- **One tap from you:** merging any PR.
- **Deliberately manual:** fixes that change real code or data тАФ compliance hours, XP ledger, charter
  preamble. These propose-and-stop so a human decides. That's a safety feature for a system holding a
  child's school records, not a gap to close.



## 8. Conventions for this system

- **Design here, build there.** This home base produces decisions and prompts. Claude Code makes the code changes, always on a branch, always reviewed before merge.
- **Inspect тЖТ validate тЖТ propose for anything touching an invariant.** Hours math, XP ledger, and the additive-hours rule are never auto-fixed. They land as a proposal in the ledger for a human call.
- **One issue ID per fix run.** Keeps PRs small and reviewable.
- **Ledger is the memory.** If it isn't in the ledger, it didn't happen. Every audit and fix updates it.
- **Environment is Claude Code web, phone-first.** Nathan rarely runs anything locally. Claude Code web executes all builds/lint/tests/git in its own environment as part of running a prompt. No prompt should ask the human to run a command, install tooling, or use a local shell. The human's actions are limited to: pasting a prompt, uploading files, and reviewing/merging PRs from the phone.
